grass in fedora-32

This page displays detail informations of the grass package. You might want go back to the main page of grass.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2020-06-26 Markus Neteler - 7.8.3-7 - added PDAL support
2020-06-21 Markus Neteler - 7.8.3-6 - disable automagic byte compilation (BZ#1847153)
2020-05-26 Markus Neteler - 7.8.3-5 - fixed wxPython for F33 (BZ#1836761)
2020-05-21 Sandro Mani - 7.8.3-4 - Rebuild (gdal)
2020-05-09 Markus Neteler - 7.8.3-3 - disabled mysql on EPEL8 due to header problem - updated PROJ package names for EPEL8
2020-05-06 Markus Neteler - 7.8.3-2 - enforce Python3 on EPEL7 - do not hardcode python version on Fedora but use macro
2020-05-05 Markus Neteler - 7.8.3 - new upstream version GRASS GIS 7.8.3
2020-03-03 Sandro Mani - 7.8.2-3 - Rebuild (gdal)
2020-01-29 Fedora Release Engineering - 7.8.2-2 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_32_Mass_Rebuild
2019-12-12 Markus Neteler - 7.8.2 - new upstream version GRASS GIS 7.8.2
